<pr_description>
BUG: Variable not defined when awaited and rendered inside a snippet
### Describe the bug

I’m using the experimental `async` flag.

When rendering an awaited variable inside a snippet — without explicitly declaring it in the snippet parameters — the console throws the following error:

```
Uncaught (in promise) ReferenceError: value is not defined
```

I’m currently on **v5.38.3**. This was working correctly in **v5.38.2**.


### Reproduction

https://stackblitz.com/edit/sveltejs-kit-template-default-ry9pp9kr?file=src%2Froutes%2F%2Bpage.svelte

    50	                                if (parent.computed) e.rune_invalid_computed_property(parent);
    51	                                name += `.${/** @type {Identifier} */ (parent.property).name}`;
    52	
    53	                                current = parent;
    54	                                parent = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.path[--i]);
    55	
    56	                                if (!is_rune(name)) {
    57	                                        if (name === '$effect.active') {
    58	                                                e.rune_renamed(parent, '$effect.active', '$effect.tracking');
    59	                                        }
    60	
    61	                                        if (name === '$state.frozen') {
    62	                                                e.rune_renamed(parent, '$state.frozen', '$state.raw');
    63	                                        }
    64	
    65	                                        if (name === '$state.is') {
    66	                                                e.rune_removed(parent, '$state.is');
    67	                                        }
    68	
    69	                                        e.rune_invalid_name(parent, name);
    70	                                }
    71	                        }
    72	
    73	                        if (parent.type !== 'CallExpression') {
    74	                                e.rune_missing_parentheses(current);
    75	                        }
    76	                }
    77	        }
    78	
    79	        let binding = context.state.scope.get(node.name);
    80	
    81	        if (!context.state.analysis.runes) {
    82	                if (node.name === '$$props') {
    83	                        context.state.analysis.uses_props = true;
    84	                }
    85	
    86	                if (node.name === '$$restProps') {
    87	                        context.state.analysis.uses_rest_props = true;
    88	                }
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        if (binding) {
    92	                if (context.state.expression) {
    93	                        context.state.expression.dependencies.add(binding);
    94	                        context.state.expression.references.add(binding);
    95	                        context.state.expression.has_state ||=
    96	                                binding.kind !== 'static' &&
    97	                                (binding.kind === 'prop' ||
    98	                                        binding.kind === 'bindable_prop' ||
    99	                                        binding.kind === 'rest_prop' ||
   100	                                        !binding.is_function()) &&
   101	                                !context.state.scope.evaluate(node).is_known;
   102	                }
   103	
   104	                if (
   105	                        context.state.analysis.runes &&
   106	                        node !== binding.node &&
   107	                        context.state.function_depth === binding.scope.function_depth &&
   108	                        // If we have $state that can be proxied or frozen and isn't re-assigned, then that means
   109	                        // it's likely not using a primitive value and thus this warning isn't that helpful.
   110	                        ((binding.kind === 'state' &&
   111	                                (binding.reassigned ||
   112	                                        (binding.initial?.type === 'CallExpression' &&
   113	                                                binding.initial.arguments.length === 1 &&
   114	                                                binding.initial.arguments[0].type !== 'SpreadElement' &&
   115	                                                !should_proxy(binding.initial.arguments[0], context.state.scope)))) ||
   116	                                binding.kind === 'raw_state' ||
   117	                                binding.kind === 'derived') &&
   118	                        // We're only concerned with reads here
   119	                        (parent.type !== 'AssignmentExpression' || parent.left !== node) &&
   120	                        parent.type !== 'UpdateExpression'
   121	                ) {
   122	                        let type = 'closure';
   123	
   124	                        let i = context.path.length;
   125	                        while (i--) {
   126	                                const parent = context.path[i];
   127	
   128	                                if (
   129	                                        parent.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' ||
   130	                                        parent.type === 'FunctionDeclaration' ||
   131	                                        parent.type === 'FunctionExpression'
   132	                                ) {
   133	                                        break;
   134	                                }
   135	
   136	                                if (
   137	                                        parent.type === 'CallExpression' &&
   138	                                        parent.arguments.includes(/** @type {any} */ (context.path[i + 1]))
   139	                                ) {
   140	                                        const rune = get_rune(parent, context.state.scope);
   141	
   142	                                        if (rune === '$state' || rune === '$state.raw') {
   143	                                                type = 'derived';
   144	                                                break;
   145	                                        }
   146	                                }
   147	                        }
   148	
   149	                        w.state_referenced_locally(node, node.name, type);
   150	                }
   151	
   152	                if (
   153	                        context.state.reactive_statement &&
   154	                        binding.scope === context.state.analysis.module.scope &&
   155	                        binding.reassigned
   156	                ) {
   157	                        w.reactive_declaration_module_script_dependency(node);
   158	                }
   159	
   160	                if (binding.metadata?.is_template_declaration && context.state.options.experimental.async) {
   161	                        let snippet_name;
   162	
   163	                        // Find out if this references a {@const ...} declaration of an implicit children snippet
   164	                        // when it is itself inside a snippet block at the same level. If so, error.
   165	                        for (let i = context.path.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
   166	                                const parent = context.path[i];
   167	                                const grand_parent = context.path[i - 1];
   168	
   169	                                if (parent.type === 'SnippetBlock') {
   170	                                        snippet_name = parent.expression.name;
   171	                                } else if (
   172	                                        snippet_name &&
   173	                                        grand_parent &&
   174	                                        parent.type === 'Fragment' &&
   175	                                        (is_component_node(grand_parent) ||
   176	                                                (grand_parent.type === 'SvelteBoundary' &&
   177	                                                        (snippet_name === 'failed' || snippet_name === 'pending')))
   178	                                ) {
   179	                                        if (
   180	                                                is_component_node(grand_parent)
   181	                                                        ? grand_parent.metadata.scopes.default === binding.scope
   182	                                                        : context.state.scopes.get(parent) === binding.scope
   183	                                        ) {
   184	                                                e.const_tag_invalid_reference(node, node.name);
   185	                                        } else {
   186	                                                break;
   187	                                        }
   188	                                }
   189	                        }
   190	                }
   191	        }
   192	}
   193

     1	/** @import { AST, Binding } from '#compiler' */
     2	/** @import { Scope } from '../../scope' */
     3	/** @import { Context } from '../types' */
     4	import { validate_block_not_empty, validate_opening_tag } from './shared/utils.js';
     5	import * as e from '../../../errors.js';
     6	
     7	/**
     8	 * @param {AST.SnippetBlock} node
     9	 * @param {Context} context
    10	 */
    11	export function SnippetBlock(node, context) {
    12	        context.state.analysis.snippets.add(node);
    13	
    14	        validate_block_not_empty(node.body, context);
    15	
    16	        if (context.state.analysis.runes) {
    17	                validate_opening_tag(node, context.state, '#');
    18	        }
    19	
    20	        for (const arg of node.parameters) {
    21	                if (arg.type === 'RestElement') {
    22	                        e.snippet_invalid_rest_parameter(arg);
    23	                }
    24	        }
    25	
    26	        context.next({ ...context.state, parent_element: null });
    27	
    28	        const can_hoist =
    29	                context.path.length === 1 &&
    30	                context.path[0].type === 'Fragment' &&
    31	                can_hoist_snippet(context.state.scope, context.state.scopes);
    32	
    33	        const name = node.expression.name;
    34	
    35	        if (can_hoist) {
    36	                const binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (context.state.scope.get(name));
    37	                context.state.analysis.module.scope.declarations.set(name, binding);
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        node.metadata.can_hoist = can_hoist;
    41	
    42	        const { path } = context;
    43	        const parent = path.at(-2);
    44	        if (!parent) return;
    45	
    46	        if (
    47	                parent.type === 'Component' &&
    48	                parent.attributes.some(
    49	                        (attribute) =>
    50	                                (attribute.type === 'Attribute' || attribute.type === 'BindDirective') &&
    51	                                attribute.name === node.expression.name
    52	                )
    53	        ) {
    54	                e.snippet_shadowing_prop(node, node.expression.name);
    55	        }
    56	
    57	        if (node.expression.name !== 'children') return;
    58	
    59	        if (
    60	                parent.type === 'Component' ||
    61	                parent.type === 'SvelteComponent' ||
    62	                parent.type === 'SvelteSelf'
    63	        ) {
    64	                if (
    65	                        parent.fragment.nodes.some(
    66	                                (node) =>
    67	                                        node.type !== 'SnippetBlock' &&
    68	                                        (node.type !== 'Text' || node.data.trim()) &&
    69	                                        node.type !== 'Comment'
    70	                        )
    71	                ) {
    72	                        e.snippet_conflict(node);
    73	                }
    74	        }
    75	}
    76	
    77	/**
    78	 * @param {Map<AST.SvelteNode, Scope>} scopes
    79	 * @param {Scope} scope
    80	 */
    81	function can_hoist_snippet(scope, scopes, visited = new Set()) {
    82	        for (const [reference] of scope.references) {
    83	                const binding = scope.get(reference);
    84	
    85	                if (!binding || binding.scope.function_depth === 0) {
    86	                        continue;
    87	                }
    88	
    89	                // ignore bindings declared inside the snippet (e.g. the snippet's own parameters)
    90	                if (binding.scope.function_depth >= scope.function_depth) {
    91	                        continue;
    92	                }
    93	
    94	                if (binding.initial?.type === 'SnippetBlock') {
    95	                        if (visited.has(binding)) continue;
    96	                        visited.add(binding);
    97	                        const snippet_scope = /** @type {Scope} */ (scopes.get(binding.initial));
    98	
    99	                        if (can_hoist_snippet(snippet_scope, scopes, visited)) {
   100	                                continue;
   101	                        }
   102	                }
   103	
   104	                return false;
   105	        }
   106	
   107	        return true;
   108	}

     1	/** @import { AssignmentPattern, BlockStatement, Expression, Identifier, Statement } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
     3	/** @import { ComponentContext } from '../types' */
     4	import { dev } from '../../../../state.js';
     5	import { extract_paths } from '../../../../utils/ast.js';
     6	import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
     7	import { get_value } from './shared/declarations.js';
     8	
     9	/**
    10	 * @param {AST.SnippetBlock} node
    11	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    12	 */
    13	export function SnippetBlock(node, context) {
    14	        // TODO hoist where possible
    15	        /** @type {(Identifier | AssignmentPattern)[]} */
    16	        const args = [b.id('$$anchor')];
    17	        const has_await = node.body.metadata.has_await || false;
    18	
    19	        /** @type {BlockStatement} */
    20	        let body;
    21	
    22	        /** @type {Statement[]} */
    23	        const declarations = [];
    24	
    25	        const transform = { ...context.state.transform };
    26	        const child_state = { ...context.state, transform };
    27	
    28	        for (let i = 0; i < node.parameters.length; i++) {
    29	                const argument = node.parameters[i];
    30	
    31	                if (!argument) continue;
    32	
    33	                if (argument.type === 'Identifier') {
    34	                        args.push(b.assignment_pattern(argument, b.id('$.noop')));
    35	                        transform[argument.name] = { read: b.call };
    36	
    37	                        continue;
    38	                }
    39	
    40	                let arg_alias = `$$arg${i}`;
    41	                args.push(b.id(arg_alias));
    42	
    43	                const { inserts, paths } = extract_paths(argument, b.maybe_call(b.id(arg_alias)));
    44	
    45	                for (const { id, value } of inserts) {
    46	                        id.name = context.state.scope.generate('$$array');
    47	                        transform[id.name] = { read: get_value };
    48	
    49	                        declarations.push(
    50	                                b.var(id, b.call('$.derived', /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(b.thunk(value)))))
    51	                        );
    52	                }
    53	
    54	                for (const path of paths) {
    55	                        const name = /** @type {Identifier} */ (path.node).name;
    56	                        const needs_derived = path.has_default_value; // to ensure that default value is only called once
    57	                        const fn = b.thunk(/** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(path.expression, child_state)));
    58	
    59	                        declarations.push(b.let(path.node, needs_derived ? b.call('$.derived_safe_equal', fn) : fn));
    60	
    61	                        transform[name] = {
    62	                                read: needs_derived ? get_value : b.call
    63	                        };
    64	
    65	                        // we need to eagerly evaluate the expression in order to hit any
    66	                        // 'Cannot access x before initialization' errors
    67	                        if (dev) {
    68	                                declarations.push(b.stmt(transform[name].read(b.id(name))));
    69	                        }
    70	                }
    71	        }
    72	        const block = /** @type {BlockStatement} */ (context.visit(node.body, child_state)).body;
    73	        body = b.block([
    74	                dev ? b.stmt(b.call('$.validate_snippet_args', b.spread(b.id('arguments')))) : b.empty,
    75	                ...declarations,
    76	                ...block
    77	        ]);
    78	
    79	        // in dev we use a FunctionExpression (not arrow function) so we can use `arguments`
    80	        let snippet = dev
    81	                ? b.call(
    82	                                '$.wrap_snippet',
    83	                                b.id(context.state.analysis.name),
    84	                                b.function(null, args, body, has_await)
    85	                        )
    86	                : b.arrow(args, body, has_await);
    87	
    88	        const declaration = b.const(node.expression, snippet);
    89	
    90	        // Top-level snippets are hoisted so they can be referenced in the `<script>`
    91	        if (context.path.length === 1 && context.path[0].type === 'Fragment') {
    92	                if (node.metadata.can_hoist) {
    93	                        context.state.module_level_snippets.push(declaration);
    94	                } else {
    95	                        context.state.instance_level_snippets.push(declaration);
    96	                }
    97	        } else {
    98	                context.state.init.push(declaration);
    99	        }
   100	}

     1	/** @import { Expression, Statement } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
     3	/** @import { ComponentContext } from '../types' */
     4	import { unwrap_optional } from '../../../../utils/ast.js';
     5	import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
     6	import { add_svelte_meta, build_expression, Memoizer } from './shared/utils.js';
     7	
     8	/**
     9	 * @param {AST.RenderTag} node
    10	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    11	 */
    12	export function RenderTag(node, context) {
    13	        context.state.template.push_comment();
    14	
    15	        const call = unwrap_optional(node.expression);
    16	
    17	        /** @type {Expression[]} */
    18	        let args = [];
    19	
    20	        const memoizer = new Memoizer();
    21	
    22	        for (let i = 0; i < call.arguments.length; i++) {
    23	                const arg = /** @type {Expression} */ (call.arguments[i]);
    24	                const metadata = node.metadata.arguments[i];
    25	
    26	                let expression = build_expression(context, arg, metadata);
    27	
    28	                if (metadata.has_await || metadata.has_call) {
    29	                        expression = b.call('$.get', memoizer.add(expression, metadata.has_await));
    30	                }
    31	
    32	                args.push(b.thunk(expression));
    33	        }
    34	
    35	        memoizer.apply();
    36	
    37	        /** @type {Statement[]} */
    38	        const statements = memoizer.deriveds(context.state.analysis.runes);
    39	
    40	        let snippet_function = build_expression(
    41	                context,
    42	                /** @type {Expression} */ (call.callee),
    43	                node.metadata.expression
    44	        );
    45	
    46	        if (node.metadata.dynamic) {
    47	                // If we have a chain expression then ensure a nullish snippet function gets turned into an empty one
    48	                if (node.expression.type === 'ChainExpression') {
    49	                        snippet_function = b.logical('??', snippet_function, b.id('$.noop'));
    50	                }
    51	
    52	                statements.push(
    53	                        add_svelte_meta(
    54	                                b.call('$.snippet', context.state.node, b.thunk(snippet_function), ...args),
    55	                                node,
    56	                                'render'
    57	                        )
    58	                );
    59	        } else {
    60	                statements.push(
    61	                        add_svelte_meta(
    62	                                (node.expression.type === 'CallExpression' ? b.call : b.maybe_call)(
    63	                                        snippet_function,
    64	                                        context.state.node,
    65	                                        ...args
    66	                                ),
    67	                                node,
    68	                                'render'
    69	                        )
    70	                );
    71	        }
    72	
    73	        const async_values = memoizer.async_values();
    74	
    75	        if (async_values) {
    76	                context.state.init.push(
    77	                        b.stmt(
    78	                                b.call(
    79	                                        '$.async',
    80	                                        context.state.node,
    81	                                        memoizer.async_values(),
    82	                                        b.arrow([context.state.node, ...memoizer.async_ids()], b.block(statements))
    83	                                )
    84	                        )
    85	                );
    86	        } else {
    87	                context.state.init.push(statements.length === 1 ? statements[0] : b.block(statements));
    88	        }
    89	}

    13	/**
    14	 * A utility for extracting complex expressions (such as call expressions)
    15	 * from templates and replacing them with `$0`, `$1` etc
    16	 */
    17	export class Memoizer {
    18	        /** @type {Array<{ id: Identifier, expression: Expression }>} */
    19	        #sync = [];
    20	
    21	        /** @type {Array<{ id: Identifier, expression: Expression }>} */
    22	        #async = [];
    23	
    24	        /**
    25	         * @param {Expression} expression
    26	         * @param {boolean} has_await
    27	         */
    28	        add(expression, has_await) {
    29	                const id = b.id('#'); // filled in later
    30	
    31	                (has_await ? this.#async : this.#sync).push({ id, expression });
    32	
    33	                return id;
    34	        }
    35	
    36	        apply() {
    37	                return [...this.#sync, ...this.#async].map((memo, i) => {
    38	                        memo.id.name = `$${i}`;
    39	                        return memo.id;
    40	                });
    41	        }
    42	
    43	        deriveds(runes = true) {
    44	                return this.#sync.map((memo) =>
    45	                        b.let(memo.id, b.call(runes ? '$.derived' : '$.derived_safe_equal', b.thunk(memo.expression)))
    46	                );
    47	        }
    48	
    49	        async_ids() {
    50	                return this.#async.map((memo) => memo.id);
    51	        }
    52	
    53	        async_values() {
    54	                if (this.#async.length === 0) return;
    55	                return b.array(this.#async.map((memo) => b.thunk(memo.expression, true)));
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        sync_values() {
    59	                if (this.#sync.length === 0) return;
    60	                return b.array(this.#sync.map((memo) => b.thunk(memo.expression)));
    61	        }
    62	}

    64	/**
    65	 * @param {Array<AST.Text | AST.ExpressionTag>} values
    66	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    67	 * @param {ComponentClientTransformState} state
    68	 * @param {(value: Expression, metadata: ExpressionMetadata) => Expression} memoize
    69	 * @returns {{ value: Expression, has_state: boolean }}
    70	 */
    71	export function build_template_chunk(
    72	        values,
    73	        context,
    74	        state = context.state,
    75	        memoize = (value, metadata) =>
    76	                metadata.has_call || metadata.has_await ? state.memoizer.add(value, metadata.has_await) : value
    77	) {
    78	        /** @type {Expression[]} */
    79	        const expressions = [];
    80	
    81	        let quasi = b.quasi('');
    82	        const quasis = [quasi];
    83	
    84	        let has_state = false;
    85	        let has_await = false;
    86	
    87	        for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    88	                const node = values[i];
    89	
    90	                if (node.type === 'Text') {
    91	                        quasi.value.cooked += node.data;
    92	                } else if (node.expression.type === 'Literal') {
    93	                        if (node.expression.value != null) {
    94	                                quasi.value.cooked += node.expression.value + '';
    95	                        }
    96	                } else if (
    97	                        node.expression.type !== 'Identifier' ||
    98	                        node.expression.name !== 'undefined' ||
    99	                        state.scope.get('undefined')
   100	                ) {
   101	                        let value = memoize(
   102	                                build_expression(context, node.expression, node.metadata.expression, state),
   103	                                node.metadata.expression
   104	                        );
   105	
   106	                        const evaluated = state.scope.evaluate(value);
   107	
   108	                        has_await ||= node.metadata.expression.has_await;
   109	                        has_state ||= has_await || (node.metadata.expression.has_state && !evaluated.is_known);
   110	
   111	                        if (values.length === 1) {
   112	                                // If we have a single expression, then pass that in directly to possibly avoid doing
   113	                                // extra work in the template_effect (instead we do the work in set_text).
   114	                                if (evaluated.is_known) {
   115	                                        value = b.literal((evaluated.value ?? '') + '');
   116	                                }
   117	
   118	                                return { value, has_state };
   119	                        }
   120	
   121	                        if (
   122	                                value.type === 'LogicalExpression' &&
   123	                                value.right.type === 'Literal' &&
   124	                                (value.operator === '??' || value.operator === '||')
   125	                        ) {
   126	                                // `foo ?? null` -=> `foo ?? ''`
   127	                                // otherwise leave the expression untouched
   128	                                if (value.right.value === null) {
   129	                                        value = { ...value, right: b.literal('') };
   130	                                }
   131	                        }
   132	
   133	                        if (evaluated.is_known) {
   134	                                quasi.value.cooked += (evaluated.value ?? '') + '';
   135	                        } else {
   136	                                if (!evaluated.is_defined) {
   137	                                        // add `?? ''` where necessary
   138	                                        value = b.logical('??', value, b.literal(''));
   139	                                }
   140	
   141	                                expressions.push(value);
   142	
   143	                                quasi = b.quasi('', i + 1 === values.length);
   144	                                quasis.push(quasi);
   145	                        }
   146	                }
   147	        }
   148	
   149	        for (const quasi of quasis) {
   150	                quasi.value.raw = sanitize_template_string(/** @type {string} */ (quasi.value.cooked));
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        const value =
   154	                expressions.length > 0
   155	                        ? b.template(quasis, expressions)
   156	                        : b.literal(/** @type {string} */ (quasi.value.cooked));
   157	
   158	        return { value, has_state };
   159	}

   161	/**
   162	 * @param {ComponentClientTransformState} state

   164	export function build_render_statement(state) {
   165	        const { memoizer } = state;
   166	
   167	        const ids = memoizer.apply();

   184	/**
   185	 * For unfortunate legacy reasons, directive names can look like this `use:a.b-c`
   186	 * This turns that string into a member expression
   187	 * @param {string} name
   188	 */
   189	export function parse_directive_name(name) {
   190	        // this allow for accessing members of an object
   191	        const parts = name.split('.');
   192	        let part = /** @type {string} */ (parts.shift());
   193	
   194	        /** @type {Identifier | MemberExpression} */
   195	        let expression = b.id(part);
   196	
   197	        while ((part = /** @type {string} */ (parts.shift()))) {
   198	                const computed = !regex_is_valid_identifier.test(part);
   199	                expression = b.member(expression, computed ? b.literal(part) : b.id(part), computed);
   200	        }
   201	
   202	        return expression;
   203	}

     2	/** @import { Context } from '../types' */

     5	/**
     6	 * @param {AwaitExpression} node
     7	 * @param {Context} context
     8	 */
     9	export function AwaitExpression(node, context) {
    10	        let suspend = context.state.ast_type === 'instance' && context.state.function_depth === 1;
    11	
    12	        if (context.state.expression) {
    13	                context.state.expression.has_await = true;
    14	
    15	                if (
    16	                        context.state.fragment &&
    17	                        // TODO there's probably a better way to do this
    18	                        context.path.some((node) => node.type === 'ConstTag')
    19	                ) {
    20	                        context.state.fragment.metadata.has_await = true;
    21	                }
    22	
    23	                suspend = true;
    24	        }
    25	
    26	        // disallow top-level `await` or `await` in template expressions
    27	        // unless a) in runes mode and b) opted into `experimental.async`

    31	                }
    32	
    33	                if (!context.state.analysis.runes) {
    34	                        e.legacy_await_invalid(node);
    35	                }
    36	        }
    37	
    38	        context.next();
    39	}

  1091	                        const parent = context.path.at(-1);
  1092	                        if (
  1093	                                parent?.type === 'FunctionDeclaration' ||
  1094	                                parent?.type === 'FunctionExpression' ||
  1095	                                parent?.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression'
  1096	                        ) {
  1097	                                // We already created a new scope for the function
  1098	                                context.next();
  1099	                        } else {
  1100	                                create_block_scope(node, context);
  1101	                        }
  1102	                },
  1103	
  1104	                ClassDeclaration(node, { state, next }) {
  1105	                        if (node.id) state.scope.declare(node.id, 'normal', 'let', node);
  1106	                        next();
  1107	                },
  1108	
  1109	                VariableDeclaration(node, { state, path, next }) {
  1110	                        const is_parent_const_tag = path.at(-1)?.type === 'ConstTag';
  1111	                        for (const declarator of node.declarations) {
  1112	                                /** @type {Binding[]} */
  1113	                                const bindings = [];
  1114	
  1115	                                state.scope.declarators.set(declarator, bindings);
  1116	
  1117	                                for (const id of extract_identifiers(declarator.id)) {
  1118	                                        const binding = state.scope.declare(
  1119	                                                id,
  1120	                                                is_parent_const_tag ? 'template' : 'normal',
  1121	                                                node.kind,
  1122	                                                declarator.init
  1123	                                        );
  1124	                                        binding.metadata = { is_template_declaration: true };
  1125	                                        bindings.push(binding);
  1126	                                }
  1127	                        }
  1128	
  1129	                        next();
  1130	                },
  1131	
  1132	                CatchClause(node, { state, next }) {
  1133	                        if (node.param) {
  1134	                                const scope = state.scope.child(true);
  1135	                                scopes.set(node, scope);
  1136	
  1137	                                for (const id of extract_identifiers(node.param)) {
  1138	                                        scope.declare(id, 'normal', 'let');
  1139	                                }
  1140	
  1141	                                next({ scope });
  1142	                        } else {
  1143	                                next();
  1144	                        }
  1145	                },
  1146	
  1147	                EachBlock(node, { state, visit }) {
  1148	                        visit(node.expression);
  1149	
  1150	                        // context and children are a new scope
  1151	                        const scope = state.scope.child();
  1152	                        scopes.set(node, scope);
  1153	
  1154	                        if (node.context) {
  1155	                                // declarations
  1156	                                for (const id of extract_identifiers(node.context)) {
  1157	                                        const binding = scope.declare(id, 'each', 'const');
  1158	
  1159	                                        let inside_rest = false;
  1160	                                        let is_rest_id = false;
  1161	                                        walk(node.context, null, {
  1162	                                                Identifier(node) {
  1163	                                                        if (inside_rest && node === id) {
  1164	                                                                is_rest_id = true;
  1165	                                                        }
  1166	                                                },
  1167	                                                RestElement(_, { next }) {
  1168	                                                        const prev = inside_rest;
  1169	                                                        inside_rest = true;
  1170	                                                        next();
  1171	                                                        inside_rest = prev;
  1172	                                                }
  1173	                                        });
  1174	
  1175	                                        binding.metadata = { inside_rest: is_rest_id };
  1176	                                }
  1177	
  1178	                                // Visit to pick up references from default initializers
  1179	                                visit(node.context, { scope });
  1180	                        }

    14	/**
    15	 * `compile` converts your `.svelte` source code into a JavaScript module that exports a component
    16	 *
    17	 * @param {string} source The component source code
    18	 * @param {CompileOptions} options The compiler options
    19	 * @returns {CompileResult}
    20	 */
    21	export function compile(source, options) {
    22	        source = remove_bom(source);
    23	        state.reset({ warning: options.warningFilter, filename: options.filename });
    24	        const validated = validate_component_options(options, '');
    25	
    26	        let parsed = _parse(source);
    27	
    28	        const { customElement: customElementOptions, ...parsed_options } = parsed.options || {};
    29	
    30	        /** @type {ValidatedCompileOptions} */
    31	        const combined_options = {
    32	                ...validated,
    33	                ...parsed_options,
    34	                customElementOptions
    35	        };
    36	
    37	        if (parsed.metadata.ts) {
    38	                parsed = {
    39	                        ...parsed,
    40	                        fragment: parsed.fragment && remove_typescript_nodes(parsed.fragment),
    41	                        instance: parsed.instance && remove_typescript_nodes(parsed.instance),
    42	                        module: parsed.module && remove_typescript_nodes(parsed.module)
    43	                };
    44	                if (combined_options.customElementOptions?.extend) {
    45	                        combined_options.customElementOptions.extend = remove_typescript_nodes(
    46	                                combined_options.customElementOptions?.extend
    47	                        );
    48	                }
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        const analysis = analyze_component(parsed, source, combined_options);
    52	        const result = transform_component(analysis, source, combined_options);
    53	        result.ast = to_public_ast(source, parsed, options.modernAst);
    54	        return result;
    55	}
    56	
    57	/**
    58	 * `compileModule` takes your JavaScript source code containing runes, and turns it into a JavaScript module.
    59	 *
    60	 * @param {string} source The component source code
    61	 * @param {ModuleCompileOptions} options
    62	 * @returns {CompileResult}
    63	 */
    64	export function compileModule(source, options) {
    65	        source = remove_bom(source);
    66	        state.reset({ warning: options.warningFilter, filename: options.filename });
    67	        const validated = validate_module_options(options, '');
    68	
    69	        const analysis = analyze_module(source, validated);
    70	        return transform_module(analysis, source, validated);
    71	}

import 'svelte/internal/disclose-version';
import 'svelte/internal/flags/async';
import * as $ from 'svelte/internal/client';

var root_1 = $.from_html(`<p> </p>`);

export default function Repro($$anchor) {
	const test = ($$anchor) => {
		var p = root_1();
		var text = $.child(p, true);

		$.reset(p);
		$.template_effect(() => $.set_text(text, value));
		$.append($$anchor, p);
	};

	$.async_body(async () => {
		let value = (await $.save(Promise.resolve('hello')))();

		if ($.aborted()) return;

		test($$anchor);
	});
}

   588	         * A map of declarators to the bindings they declare
   589	         * @type {Map<VariableDeclarator | AST.LetDirective, Binding[]>}
   590	         */
   591	        declarators = new Map();
   592	
   593	        /**
   594	         * A set of all the names referenced with this scope
   595	         * — useful for generating unique names
   596	         * @type {Map<string, { node: Identifier; path: AST.SvelteNode[] }[]>}
   597	         */
   598	        references = new Map();
   599	
   600	        /**
   601	         * The scope depth allows us to determine if a state variable is referenced in its own scope,
   602	         * which is usually an error. Block statements do not increase this value
   603	         */
   604	        function_depth = 0;
   605	
   606	        /**
   607	         * If tracing of reactive dependencies is enabled for this scope
   608	         * @type {null | Expression}
   609	         */
   610	        tracing = null;
   611	
   612	        /**
   613	         *
   614	         * @param {ScopeRoot} root
   615	         * @param {Scope | null} parent
   616	         * @param {boolean} porous
   617	         */
   618	        constructor(root, parent, porous) {
   619	                this.root = root;
   620	                this.parent = parent;
   621	                this.#porous = porous;
   622	                this.function_depth = parent ? parent.function_depth + (porous ? 0 : 1) : 0;
   623	        }
   624	
   625	        /**
   626	         * @param {Identifier} node
   627	         * @param {Binding['kind']} kind
   628	         * @param {DeclarationKind} declaration_kind
   629	         * @param {null | Expression | FunctionDeclaration | ClassDeclaration | ImportDeclaration | AST.EachBlock | AST.SnippetBlock} initial
   630	         * @returns {Binding}
   631	         */
   632	        declare(node, kind, declaration_kind, initial = null) {
   633	                if (this.parent) {
   634	                        if (declaration_kind === 'var' && this.#porous) {
   635	                                return this.parent.declare(node, kind, declaration_kind);
   636	                        }
   637	
   638	                        if (declaration_kind === 'import') {
   639	                                return this.parent.declare(node, kind, declaration_kind, initial);
   640	                        }
   641	                }
   642	
   643	                if (this.declarations.has(node.name)) {
   644	                        const binding = this.declarations.get(node.name);
   645	                        if (binding && binding.declaration_kind !== 'var' && declaration_kind !== 'var') {
   646	                                // This also errors on function types, but that's arguably a good thing
   647	                                // declaring function twice is also caught by acorn in the parse phase
   648	                                e.declaration_duplicate(node, node.name);
   649	                        }
   650	                }
   651	
   652	                const binding = new Binding(this, node, kind, declaration_kind, initial);
   653	
   654	                validate_identifier_name(binding, this.function_depth);
   655	
   656	                this.declarations.set(node.name, binding);
   657	                this.root.conflicts.add(node.name);
   658	                return binding;
   659	        }
   660	
   661	        child(porous = false) {
   662	                return new Scope(this.root, this, porous);
   663	        }
   664	
   665	        /**
   666	         * @param {string} preferred_name
   667	         * @returns {string}
   668	         */
   669	        generate(preferred_name) {
   670	                if (this.#porous) {
   671	                        return /** @type {Scope} */ (this.parent).generate(preferred_name);
   672	                }
   673	
   674	                preferred_name = preferred_name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_$]/g, '_').replace(/^[0-9]/, '_');
   675	                let name = preferred_name;
   676	                let n = 1;
   677	
   678	                while (
   679	                        this.references.has(name) ||
   680	                        this.declarations.has(name) ||
   681	                        this.root.conflicts.has(name) ||
   682	                        is_reserved(name)
   683	                ) {
   684	                        name = `${preferred_name}_${n++}`;
   685	                }
   686	
   687	                this.references.set(name, []);
   688	                this.root.conflicts.add(name);
   689	                return name;
   690	        }
   691	
   692	        /**
   693	         * @param {string} name
   694	         * @returns {Binding | null}
   695	         */
   696	        get(name) {
   697	                return this.declarations.get(name) ?? this.parent?.get(name) ?? null;
   698	        }
   699	
   700	        /**
   701	         * @param {VariableDeclarator | AST.LetDirective} node
   702	         * @returns {Binding[]}
   703	         */
   704	        get_bindings(node) {
   705	                const bindings = this.declarators.get(node);
   706	                if (!bindings) {
   707	                        throw new Error('No binding found for declarator');
   708	                }
   709	                return bindings;
   710	        }
   711	
   712	        /**
   713	         * @param {string} name
   714	         * @returns {Scope | null}
   715	         */
   716	        owner(name) {
   717	                return this.declarations.has(name) ? this : this.parent && this.parent.owner(name);
   718	        }
   719	
   720	        /**

    64	        function push_unique(id) {

   146	export function build_hoisted_params(node, context) {
   147	        const hoisted_params = get_hoisted_params(node, context);
   148	        node.metadata.hoisted_params = hoisted_params;
   149	
   150	        /** @type {Pattern[]} */
   151	        const params = [];
   152	
   153	        if (node.params.length === 0) {
   154	                if (hoisted_params.length > 0) {
   155	                        // For the event object
   156	                        params.push(b.id(context.state.scope.generate('_')));
   157	                }
   158	        } else {
   159	                for (const param of node.params) {
   160	                        params.push(/** @type {Pattern} */ (context.visit(param)));
   161	                }
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        params.push(...hoisted_params);
   165	        return params;
   166	}

    27	 * @param {Array<() => Promise<any>>} async
    28	 * @param {(values: Value[]) => any} fn
    29	 */
    30	export function flatten(sync, async, fn) {
    31	        const d = is_runes() ? derived : derived_safe_equal;
    32	
    33	        if (async.length === 0) {
    34	                fn(sync.map(d));
    35	                return;
    36	        }
    37	
    38	        var batch = current_batch;
    39	        var parent = /** @type {Effect} */ (active_effect);
    40	
    41	        var restore = capture();
    42	        var boundary = get_pending_boundary();
    43	
    44	        Promise.all(async.map((expression) => async_derived(expression)))
    45	                .then((result) => {
    46	                        batch?.activate();
    47	
    48	                        restore();
    49	
    50	                        try {
    51	                                fn([...sync.map(d), ...result]);
    52	                        } catch (error) {
    53	                                // ignore errors in blocks that have already been destroyed
    54	                                if ((parent.f & DESTROYED) === 0) {
    55	                                        invoke_error_boundary(error, parent);
    56	                                }

    61	                })
    62	                .catch((error) => {

    64	                });
    65	}
    66	
    67	/**
    68	 * Captures the current effect context so that we can restore it after
    69	 * some asynchronous work has happened (so that e.g. `await a + b`
    70	 * causes `b` to be registered as a dependency).
    71	 */
    72	function capture() {
    73	        var previous_effect = active_effect;
    74	        var previous_reaction = active_reaction;
    75	        var previous_component_context = component_context;
    76	
    77	        return function restore() {
    78	                set_active_effect(previous_effect);
    79	                set_active_reaction(previous_reaction);
    80	                set_component_context(previous_component_context);
    81	
    82	                if (DEV) {
    83	                        set_from_async_derived(null);
    84	                }
    85	        };
    86	}
    87	
    88	/**
    89	 * Wraps an `await` expression in such a way that the effect context that was
    90	 * active before the expression evaluated can be reapplied afterwards —
    91	 * `await a + b` becomes `(await $.save(a))() + b`
    92	 * @template T
    93	 * @param {Promise<T>} promise
    94	 * @returns {Promise<() => T>}
    95	 */
    96	export async function save(promise) {
    97	        var restore = capture();
    98	        var value = await promise;
    99	
   100	        return () => {
   101	                restore();
   102	                return value;
   103	        };
   104	}
   105	
   106	/**
   107	 * Reset `current_async_effect` after the `promise` resolves, so
   108	 * that we can emit `await_reactivity_loss` warnings
   109	 * @template T
   110	 * @param {Promise<T>} promise
   111	 * @returns {Promise<() => T>}
   112	 */
   113	export async function track_reactivity_loss(promise) {
   114	        var previous_async_effect = current_async_effect;
   115	        var value = await promise;
   116	
   117	        return () => {
   118	                set_from_async_derived(previous_async_effect);
   119	                return value;
   120	        };
   121	}
   122	
   123	/**
   124	 * Used in `for await` loops in DEV, so
   125	 * that we can emit `await_reactivity_loss` warnings
   126	 * after each `async_iterator` result resolves and
   127	 * after the `async_iterator` return resolves (if it runs)
   128	 * @template T
   129	 * @template TReturn
   130	 * @param {Iterable<T> | AsyncIterable<T>} iterable
   131	 * @returns {AsyncGenerator<T, TReturn | undefined>}
   132	 */
   133	export async function* for_await_track_reactivity_loss(iterable) {
   134	        // This is based on the algorithms described in ECMA-262:
   135	        // ForIn/OfBodyEvaluation
   136	        // https://tc39.es/ecma262/multipage/ecmascript-language-statements-and-declarations.html#sec-runtime-semantics-forin-div-ofbodyevaluation-lhs-stmt-iterator-lhskind-labelset
   137	        // AsyncIteratorClose
   138	        // https://tc39.es/ecma262/multipage/abstract-operations.html#sec-asynciteratorclose
   139	
   140	        /** @type {AsyncIterator<T, TReturn>} */
   141	        // @ts-ignore
   142	        const iterator = iterable[Symbol.asyncIterator]?.() ?? iterable[Symbol.iterator]?.();
   143	
   144	        if (iterator === undefined) {
   145	                throw new TypeError('value is not async iterable');
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        /** Whether the completion of the iterator was "normal", meaning it wasn't ended via `break` or a similar method */
   149	        let normal_completion = false;
   150	        try {
   151	                while (true) {
   152	                        const { done, value } = (await track_reactivity_loss(iterator.next()))();
   153	                        if (done) {
   154	                                normal_completion = true;
   155	                                break;
   156	                        }
   157	                        yield value;
   158	                }
   159	        } finally {
   160	                // If the iterator had a normal completion and `return` is defined on the iterator, call it and return the value
   161	                if (normal_completion && iterator.return !== undefined) {
   162	                        // eslint-disable-next-line no-unsafe-finally
   163	                        return /** @type {TReturn} */ ((await track_reactivity_loss(iterator.return()))().value);
   164	                }
   165	        }
   166	}
   167	
   168	export function unset_context() {
   169	        set_active_effect(null);
   170	        set_active_reaction(null);
   171	        set_component_context(null);
   172	        if (DEV) set_from_async_derived(null);
   173	}

   175	/**

   177	 */
   178	export async function async_body(fn) {
   179	        const unsuspend = suspend();
   180	        const active = /** @type {Effect} */ (active_effect);
   181	
   182	        try {
   183	                await fn();

   187	                }
   188	        } finally {
   189	                unsuspend();
   190	        }

    41	        );
    42	
    43	        if (hoisted.length === 0 && trimmed.length === 0) {
    44	                return b.block([]);
    45	        }
    46	
    47	        const is_single_element = trimmed.length === 1 && trimmed[0].type === 'RegularElement';
    48	        const is_single_child_not_needing_template =
    49	                trimmed.length === 1 &&
    50	                (trimmed[0].type === 'SvelteFragment' || trimmed[0].type === 'TitleElement');
    51	        const has_await = context.state.init !== null && (node.metadata.has_await || false);
    52	
    53	        const template_name = context.state.scope.root.unique('root'); // TODO infer name from parent
    54	
    55	        /** @type {Statement[]} */
    56	        const body = [];
    57	
    58	        /** @type {Statement | undefined} */
    59	        let close = undefined;
    60	
    61	        /** @type {ComponentClientTransformState} */
    62	        const state = {
    63	                ...context.state,
    64	                init: [],
    65	                consts: [],
    66	                update: [],
    67	                after_update: [],
    68	                memoizer: new Memoizer(),
    69	                template: new Template(),
    70	                transform: { ...context.state.transform },
    71	                metadata: {
    72	                        namespace,
    73	                        bound_contenteditable: context.state.metadata.bound_contenteditable
    74	                }
    75	        };
    76	
    77	        for (const node of hoisted) {
    78	                context.visit(node, state);
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        if (is_single_element) {
    82	                const element = /** @type {AST.RegularElement} */ (trimmed[0]);
    83	
    84	                const id = b.id(context.state.scope.generate(element.name));
    85	
    86	                context.visit(element, {
    87	                        ...state,
    88	                        node: id
    89	                });
    90	
    91	                let flags = state.template.needs_import_node ? TEMPLATE_USE_IMPORT_NODE : undefined;
    92	
    93	                const template = transform_template(state, namespace, flags);
    94	                state.hoisted.push(b.var(template_name, template));
    95	
    96	                state.init.unshift(b.var(id, b.call(template_name)));
    97	                close = b.stmt(b.call('$.append', b.id('$$anchor'), id));
    98	        } else if (is_single_child_not_needing_template) {
    99	                context.visit(trimmed[0], state);
   100	        } else if (trimmed.length === 1 && trimmed[0].type === 'Text') {
   101	                const id = b.id(context.state.scope.generate('text'));
   102	                state.init.unshift(b.var(id, b.call('$.text', b.literal(trimmed[0].data))));
   103	                close = b.stmt(b.call('$.append', b.id('$$anchor'), id));
   104	        } else if (trimmed.length > 0) {
   105	                const id = b.id(context.state.scope.generate('fragment'));
   106	
   107	                const use_space_template =
   108	                        trimmed.some((node) => node.type === 'ExpressionTag') &&
   109	                        trimmed.every((node) => node.type === 'Text' || node.type === 'ExpressionTag');
   110	
   111	                if (use_space_template) {
   112	                        // special case — we can use `$.text` instead of creating a unique template
   113	                        const id = b.id(context.state.scope.generate('text'));
   114	
   115	                        process_children(trimmed, () => id, false, {
   116	                                ...context,
   117	                                state
   118	                        });
   119	
   120	                        state.init.unshift(b.var(id, b.call('$.text')));
   121	                        close = b.stmt(b.call('$.append', b.id('$$anchor'), id));
   122	                } else {
   123	                        if (is_standalone) {
   124	                                // no need to create a template, we can just use the existing block's anchor
   125	                                process_children(trimmed, () => b.id('$$anchor'), false, { ...context, state });
   126	                        } else {
   127	                                /** @type {(is_text: boolean) => Expression} */
   128	                                const expression = (is_text) => b.call('$.first_child', id, is_text && b.true);
   129	
   130	                                process_children(trimmed, expression, false, { ...context, state });
   131	
   132	                                let flags = TEMPLATE_FRAGMENT;
   133	
   134	                                if (state.template.needs_import_node) {
   135	                                        flags |= TEMPLATE_USE_IMPORT_NODE;
   136	                                }
   137	
   138	                                if (state.template.nodes.length === 1 && state.template.nodes[0].type === 'comment') {
   139	                                        // special case — we can use `$.comment` instead of creating a unique template
   140	                                        state.init.unshift(b.var(id, b.call('$.comment')));
   141	                                } else {
   142	                                        const template = transform_template(state, namespace, flags);
   143	                                        state.hoisted.push(b.var(template_name, template));
   144	
   145	                                        state.init.unshift(b.var(id, b.call(template_name)));
   146	                                }
   147	
   148	                                close = b.stmt(b.call('$.append', b.id('$$anchor'), id));
   149	                        }
   150	                }
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        body.push(...state.consts);
   154	
   155	        if (has_await) {
   156	                body.push(b.if(b.call('$.aborted'), b.return()));
   157	        }
   158	
   159	        if (is_text_first) {
   160	                // skip over inserted comment
   161	                body.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.next')));
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        body.push(...state.init);
   165	
   166	        if (state.update.length > 0) {
   167	                body.push(build_render_statement(state));
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        body.push(...state.after_update);
   171	
   172	        if (close !== undefined) {
   173	                // It's important that close is the last statement in the block, as any previous statements
   174	                // could contain element insertions into the template, which the close statement needs to
   175	                // know of when constructing the list of current inner elements.
   176	                body.push(close);
   177	        }
   178	
   179	        if (has_await) {
   180	                return b.block([b.stmt(b.call('$.async_body', b.arrow([], b.block(body), true)))]);
   181	        } else {
   182	                return b.block(body);
   183	        }
   184	}
   185

    91	        /** @type {ComponentServerTransformState} */

   181	
   182	                const rest = template.body.filter(
   183	                        // @ts-expect-error
   184	                        (node) => node.type !== 'FunctionDeclaration' || !node.___snippet
   185	                );
   186	
   187	                template.body = [
   188	                        ...snippets,
   189	                        b.let('$$settled', b.true),
   190	                        b.let('$$inner_payload'),
   191	                        b.function_declaration(
   192	                                b.id('$$render_inner'),
   193	                                [b.id('$$payload')],
   194	                                b.block(/** @type {Statement[]} */ (rest))
   195	                        ),
   196	                        b.do_while(
   197	                                b.unary('!', b.id('$$settled')),
   198	                                b.block([
   199	                                        b.stmt(b.assignment('=', b.id('$$settled'), b.true)),
   200	                                        b.stmt(
   201	                                                b.assignment('=', b.id('$$inner_payload'), b.call('$.copy_payload', b.id('$$payload')))
   202	                                        ),
   203	                                        b.stmt(b.call('$$render_inner', b.id('$$inner_payload')))
   204	                                ])
   205	                        ),
   206	                        b.stmt(b.call('$.assign_payload', b.id('$$payload'), b.id('$$inner_payload')))
   207	                ];
   208	        }
   209	
   210	        if (
   211	                [...analysis.instance.scope.declarations.values()].some(
   212	                        (binding) => binding.kind === 'store_sub'
   213	                )
   214	        ) {
   215	                instance.body.unshift(b.var('$$store_subs'));
   216	                template.body.push(
   217	                        b.if(b.id('$$store_subs'), b.stmt(b.call('$.unsubscribe_stores', b.id('$$store_subs'))))
   218	                );
   219	        }
   220	
   221	        // Propagate values of bound props upwards if they're undefined in the parent and have a value.
   222	        // Don't do this as part of the props retrieval because people could eagerly mutate the prop in the instance script.
   223	        /** @type {Property[]} */
   224	        const props = [];
   225	
   226	        for (const [name, binding] of analysis.instance.scope.declarations) {
   227	                if (binding.kind === 'bindable_prop' && !name.startsWith('$$')) {
   228	                        props.push(b.init(binding.prop_alias ?? name, b.id(name)));
   229	                }
   230	        }
   231	
   232	        for (const { name, alias } of analysis.exports) {
   233	                props.push(b.init(alias ?? name, b.id(name)));
   234	        }
   235	
   236	        if (props.length > 0) {
   237	                // This has no effect in runes mode other than throwing an error when someone passes
   238	                // undefined to a binding that has a default value.
   239	                template.body.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.bind_props', b.id('$$props'), b.object(props))));
   240	        }
   241	
   242	        const component_block = b.block([
   243	                .../** @type {Statement[]} */ (instance.body),
   244	                .../** @type {Statement[]} */ (template.body)
   245	        ]);
   246	
   247	        // trick esrap into including comments
   248	        component_block.loc = instance.loc;
   249	
   250	        if (analysis.props_id) {
   251	                // need to be placed on first line of the component for hydration
   252	                component_block.body.unshift(
   253	                        b.const(analysis.props_id, b.call('$.props_id', b.id('$$payload')))
   254	                );
   255	        }

   257	        let should_inject_context = dev || analysis.needs_context;

+        /** @type {ComponentClientTransformState} */
+        const state = {
+                analysis,
+                options,
+                scope: analysis.module.scope,
+                scopes: analysis.module.scopes,
+                is_instance: false,
+                hoisted: [b.import_all('$', 'svelte/internal/client')],
+                node: /** @type {any} */ (null), // populated by the root node
+                legacy_reactive_imports: [],
+                legacy_reactive_statements: new Map(),
+                metadata: {
+                        namespace: options.namespace,
+                        bound_contenteditable: false
+                },
+                events: new Set(),
+                preserve_whitespace: options.preserveWhitespace,
+                state_fields: new Map(),
+                transform: {},
+                in_constructor: false,
+                in_derived: false,
+                instance_level_snippets: [],
+                module_level_snippets: [],
+
+                // these are set inside the `Fragment` visitor, and cannot be used until then
+                init: /** @type {any} */ (null),
+                consts: /** @type {any} */ (null),
+                update: /** @type {any} */ (null),
+                after_update: /** @type {any} */ (null),
+                template: /** @type {any} */ (null),
+                memoizer: /** @type {any} */ (null)
+        };
+
+        const module = /** @type {ESTree.Program} */ (
+                walk(/** @type {AST.SvelteNode} */ (analysis.module.ast), state, visitors)
+        );
+
+        const instance_state = {
+                ...state,
+                transform: { ...state.transform },
+                scope: analysis.instance.scope,
+                scopes: analysis.instance.scopes,
+                is_instance: true
+        };
+

+                walk(/** @type {AST.SvelteNode} */ (analysis.instance.ast), instance_state, visitors)
+        );
+

+                        /** @type {AST.SvelteNode} */ (analysis.template.ast),
+                        {

+        const legacy_reactive_declarations = [];
+
+        let needs_store_cleanup = false;
+
+        for (const [name, binding] of analysis.instance.scope.declarations) {
+                if (binding.kind === 'legacy_reactive') {
+                        legacy_reactive_declarations.push(
+                                b.const(
+                                        name,

+                                )
+                        );
+                }
+                if (binding.kind === 'store_sub') {
+                        if (store_setup.length === 0) {
+                                needs_store_cleanup = true;
+                                store_init = b.const(
+                                        b.array_pattern([b.id('$$stores'), b.id('$$cleanup')]),
+                                        b.call('$.setup_stores')
+                                );

+
+                        // We're creating an arrow function that gets the store value which minifies better for two or more references
+                        const store_reference = build_getter(b.id(name.slice(1)), instance_state);

+                }
+        }
+
+        for (const [node] of analysis.reactive_statements) {

+                if (statement === undefined) {

+
+        if (analysis.reactive_statements.size > 0) {

+
+        /**
+         * Used to store the group nodes

+        /** @type {Array<ESTree.Property | ESTree.SpreadElement>} */
+        const component_returned_object = analysis.exports.flatMap(({ name, alias }) => {
+                const binding = instance_state.scope.get(name);

+

+        if (dev) push_args.push(b.id(analysis.name));
+
+        let component_block = b.block([
+                store_init,
+                ...store_setup,

+        if (analysis.instance.has_await) {

+        const should_inject_context =

+                component_returned_object.length > 0;

+        let should_inject_props =
+                should_inject_context ||

+                analysis.slot_names.size > 0;

+        // trick esrap into including comments

+        // we want the cleanup function for the stores to run as the very last thing

+                } else {

+                }

+
+        if (needs_store_cleanup) {
+                component_block.body.push(b.stmt(b.call('$$cleanup')));

+                }
+        }
+
+        if (analysis.uses_rest_props) {

+                        if (binding.kind === 'bindable_prop') named_props.push(binding.prop_alias ?? name);

+                        )
+                );
+        }
+
+        if (analysis.uses_slots) {
+                component_block.body.unshift(b.const('$$slots', b.call('$.sanitize_slots', b.id('$$props'))));
+        }
+
+        // Merge hoisted statements into module body.

+        const imports = [];

+        let body = [];
+
+        for (const entry of [...module.body, ...state.hoisted]) {
+                if (entry.type === 'ImportDeclaration') {
+                        imports.push(entry);
+                } else {
+                        body.push(entry);
+                }
+        }
+
+        body = [...imports, ...state.module_level_snippets, ...body];
+
+        const component = b.function_declaration(
+                b.id(analysis.name),
+                should_inject_props ? [b.id('$$anchor'), b.id('$$props')] : [b.id('$$anchor')],

+
+        if (options.hmr) {

+

+                const accept_fn_body = [
+                        b.stmt(b.assignment('=', b.member(incoming, 'source'), b.member(existing, 'source'))),
+                        b.stmt(b.call('$.set', b.member(existing, 'source'), b.member(incoming, 'original')))
+                ];
+
+                if (analysis.css.hash) {
+                        // remove existing `<style>` element, in case CSS changed
+                        accept_fn_body.unshift(b.stmt(b.call('$.cleanup_styles', b.literal(analysis.css.hash))));
+                }
+
+                const hmr = b.block([
+                        b.stmt(b.assignment('=', id, b.call('$.hmr', id, b.thunk(b.member(existing, 'source'))))),
+
+                        b.stmt(b.call('import.meta.hot.accept', b.arrow([b.id('module')], b.block(accept_fn_body))))
+                ]);
+
+                body.push(component, b.if(b.id('import.meta.hot'), hmr), b.export_default(b.id(analysis.name)));
+        } else {
+                body.push(b.export_default(component));
+        }
+
+        if (dev) {
+                // add `App[$.FILENAME] = 'App.svelte'` so that we can print useful messages later
+                body.unshift(
+                        b.stmt(
+                                b.assignment('=', b.member(b.id(analysis.name), '$.FILENAME', true), b.literal(filename))
+                        )
+                );
+        }
+
+        if (options.experimental.async) {
+                body.unshift(b.imports([], 'svelte/internal/flags/async'));
+        }
+
+        if (!analysis.runes) {
+                body.unshift(b.imports([], 'svelte/internal/flags/legacy'));
+        }
+
+        if (analysis.tracing) {
+                body.unshift(b.imports([], 'svelte/internal/flags/tracing'));
+        }
+
+        if (options.discloseVersion) {
+                body.unshift(b.imports([], 'svelte/internal/disclose-version'));
+        }
+
+        if (options.compatibility.componentApi === 4) {
+                body.unshift(b.imports([['createClassComponent', '$$_createClassComponent']], 'svelte/legacy'));
+                component_block.body.unshift(
+                        b.if(
+                                b.id('new.target'),
+                                b.return(
+                                        b.call(
+                                                '$$_createClassComponent',
+                                                // When called with new, the first argument is the constructor options
+                                                b.object([b.init('component', b.id(analysis.name)), b.spread(b.id('$$anchor'))])
+                                        )
+                                )
+                        )
+                );
+        } else if (dev) {
+                component_block.body.unshift(b.stmt(b.call('$.check_target', b.id('new.target'))));
+        }
+
+        if (analysis.props_id) {
+                // need to be placed on first line of the component for hydration
+                component_block.body.unshift(b.const(analysis.props_id, b.call('$.props_id')));
+        }
+
+        if (state.events.size > 0) {
+                body.push(
+                        b.stmt(b.call('$.delegate', b.array(Array.from(state.events).map((name) => b.literal(name)))))
+                );
+        }
+
+        const ce = options.customElementOptions ?? options.customElement;
+
+        if (ce) {
+                const ce_props = typeof ce === 'boolean' ? {} : ce.props || {};
+
+                /** @type {ESTree.Property[]} */
+                const props_str = [];
+
+                for (const [name, prop_def] of Object.entries(ce_props)) {
+                        const binding = analysis.instance.scope.get(name);
+                        const key = binding?.prop_alias ?? name;
+
+                        if (
+                                !prop_def.type &&
+                                binding?.initial?.type === 'Literal' &&
+                                typeof binding?.initial.value === 'boolean'
+                        ) {
+                                prop_def.type = 'Boolean';
+                        }
+
+                        const value = b.object(
+                                /** @type {ESTree.Property[]} */ (
+                                        [
+                                                prop_def.attribute ? b.init('attribute', b.literal(prop_def.attribute)) : undefined,
+                                                prop_def.reflect ? b.init('reflect', b.true) : undefined,
+                                                prop_def.type ? b.init('type', b.literal(prop_def.type)) : undefined
+                                        ].filter(Boolean)
+                                )
+                        );
+
+                        props_str.push(b.init(key, value));
+                }
+
+                for (const [name, binding] of properties) {
+                        const key = binding.prop_alias ?? name;
+                        if (ce_props[key]) continue;
+
+                        props_str.push(b.init(key, b.object([])));
+                }
+
+                const slots_str = b.array([...analysis.slot_names.keys()].map((name) => b.literal(name)));
+                const accessors_str = b.array(
+                        analysis.exports.map(({ name, alias }) => b.literal(alias ?? name))
+                );
+                const use_shadow_dom = typeof ce === 'boolean' || ce.shadow !== 'none' ? true : false;
+
+                const create_ce = b.call(
+                        '$.create_custom_element',
+                        b.id(analysis.name),
+                        b.object(props_str),
+                        slots_str,
+                        accessors_str,
+                        b.literal(use_shadow_dom),
+                        /** @type {any} */ (typeof ce !== 'boolean' ? ce.extend : undefined)
+                );
+
+                // If a tag name is provided, call `customElements.define`, otherwise leave to the user
+                if (typeof ce !== 'boolean' && typeof ce.tag === 'string') {
+                        const define = b.stmt(b.call('customElements.define', b.literal(ce.tag), create_ce));
+
+                        if (options.hmr) {
+                                body.push(
+                                        b.if(b.binary('==', b.call('customElements.get', b.literal(ce.tag)), b.null), define)
+                                );
+                        } else {
+                                body.push(define);
+                        }
+                } else {
+                        body.push(b.stmt(create_ce));
+                }
+        }
+
+        return {
+                type: 'Program',
+                sourceType: 'module',
+                body
+        };
 }

+        }
+

+                type: 'Program',
+                sourceType: 'module',
+                body: [...body, ...module.body]
+        };
 }
